###Intro###
country_event = {
	id = tram.intro
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.intro"
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = tram.800 hours = 1 }
			country_event = { id = tram.3 days = 1411 random_days = 100 }
			RUS = { country_event = { id = tram.4 days = 1411 random_days = 100 } }
			country_event = { id = tram_crisis_1936.1 days = 85 random_days = 35 }
			country_event = { id = tram_crisis_1936.3 days = 130 random_days = 35 }
			country_event = { id = tram_crisis_1936.4 days = 170 random_days = 35 }
			RUS = {
				country_event = { id = tram_crisis_1937.1 days = 285 random_days = 15 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_ai = yes }
				country_event = portrait_picker.2
			}
		}
	}
	title = tram.intro.t
	desc = tram.intro.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.intro.a
		country_event = { id = tram.992 days = 2 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = trammlad.147
				days = 40
			}
			country_event = {
				id = tram.993
				days = 20
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.intro.b
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		country_event = { id = tram.992 days = 2 }
		country_event = tram.999
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = trammlad.147
				days = 10
			}
			country_event = {
				id = tram.993
				days = 20
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.994001
	immediate = {
		annex_country = { target = SIB transfer_troops = yes }
	}
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		has_country_leader = {
			name = "Ivan Lavrov"
			ruling_only = yes
		}
		SIB = {
			exists = yes
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Ivan Lavrov"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 } 
	fire_only_once = yes
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.994002
	hidden = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		has_global_flag = RCW_begun
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RCW_over }
		RUS = { exists = no }
		RRF = { exists = no }
		WRA = { exists = no }
		RVA = { exists = no }
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.994002.a
		RUS = { clr_country_flag = soviet_speaking_tag }
		set_global_flag = RCW_over
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_rrf_state = yes
					state = 821
					state = 880
					state = 209
					state = 210
					state = 1287
					state = 1290
					state = 1289
					state = 1288
					state = 1291
				}
			}
			add_core_of = RUS
			remove_core_of = RRF
			remove_core_of = WRA
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Diterikhs dies
	id = tram.2
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.2" 
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = tram.265 days = 90 }
		}
	}
	title = tram.2.t
	desc = tram.2.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRM_diterikhs
	
	trigger = {
		RUS_russian_monarch = yes
		TRM_do_rovs_in_power = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.2.a
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 505058 }			
			remove_unit_leader = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		country_event = tram.262
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.2.b
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 505058 }			
			remove_unit_leader = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead
		remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRM_Vladimir_Gantimurov_sec_ade }
			country_event = tram.264
		}
		else = {
			country_event = tram.263
		}
	}
}
country_event = { #Diterikhs dies
	id = tram.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.3" }
	title = tram.2.t
	desc = tram.3.d
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		TRM_do_rovs_in_power = no
		NOT = { has_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead }
		has_unit_leader = 505058
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_TRM_diterikhs
	
	option = {
		name = tram.3.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_power_balance = { id = TRM_power_balance } }
			add_power_balance_value = { id = TRM_power_balance value = -0.15 }
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = -0.01
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 505058 }			
			remove_unit_leader = yes
		}
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 404 }
			promote_to_marshal = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Vladimir Kappel"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/RUS/Portrait_RUS_Vladimir_Kappel.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = junta_subtype
				traits = { TRM_voievode }
			}
		}	
		set_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead
	}
}
country_event = { #Diterikhs dies
	id = tram.4
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.4" }
	title = tram.2.t

	}

	option = {
		name = tram.3.a

		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 505058 }			
			remove_unit_leader = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = Mikhail_Diterikhs_dead
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.6" }
	title = tram.6.t
	desc = tram.6.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Demands
		name = tram.6.a
		add_stability = 0.1
		set_global_flag = TRM_siberia_panic
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = TRM_Siberian_Insurgency
		SOV = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.22
				days = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.13
				days = 75
			}
		}
	}

}

country_event = {
	id = tram.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.10" }
	title = tram.10.t
	desc = tram.10.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.10.a
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_siberia = yes
				NOT = { 
					is_core_of = TRM 
					is_core_of = YAK
					is_core_of = BRY
				}
			}
			add_compliance = 15
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.08
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TRM_has_japanese_influence = yes }
			JAP = { country_event = tram.42 }
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = tram.13

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Demands

		clr_global_flag = TRM_siberia_panic
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.24
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.24" }
	title = tram.24.t
	desc = tram.24.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.24.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = RUS
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = {
				id = russianews.7
				days = 1
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = RUS }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.24.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		RUS = {
			transfer_state = 565
			transfer_state = 563
			transfer_state = 564
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = paternal_autocrat
				has_country_flag = TRM_oblastniki_operate
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.15
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.25
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.25" }
	title = tram.25.t
	desc = tram.25.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.25.a
		TRM = {
			transfer_state = 566
			566 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			transfer_state = 644
			644 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
			transfer_state = 1202
			1202 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = TRM_control_FE
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram.42
					days = 7
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Japanese reaction on TRM expands
	id = tram.42
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.42" }
	title = tram.42.t
	desc = tram.42.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.42.a
		ai_chance = { # Do nothing
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = TRM_path 
					option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Remove government
		name = tram.42.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 5
		}
		TRM = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.48
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Replace HOS - TRM event
	id = tram.48
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.48" }
	title = tram.48.t
	desc = tram.48.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		ai_chance = { #Submit
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = DEFAULT }
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.48.a
		JAP = { country_event = tram.49 }
	}
	option = { #Break away
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_YUI }

				SUPPORT_1 = { localization_key = support_battalion_tt NAME = assault_battalion ICON = GFX_unit_assault_battalion_icon_small }

		}
		else = {

				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "division_template = \"Druzhina Svyatogo Kresta\" start_experience_factor = 0.2"
					owner = ROOT
					count = TRM_brigade_count
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_power_balance = { id = TRM_power_balance } }
			add_power_balance_value = { id = TRM_power_balance value = 0.05 }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { TRM_is_legitimate_state = yes }
			TRM_Increase_ROVS_Support = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram.61.b
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = -0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_power_balance = { id = TRM_power_balance } }
			add_power_balance_value = { id = TRM_power_balance value = -0.05 }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { TRM_is_legitimate_state = yes }
			TRM_Decrease_ROVS_Support = yes
		}
	}	
}

###Non-Kolchak TRM try to find support from Russia in war of independence with Japan###
country_event = {
	id = tram.92
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.92" }
	title = tram.92.t
	desc = tram.92.d
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		has_war_with = JAP
		country_exists = RUS
		NOT = { controls_state = 1246 }
		NOT = { controls_state = 408 }
		has_socialist_government = no
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				ruling_only = yes
				name = "Aleksandr Kolchak"
			}
		}
		RUS = { has_socialist_government = no }
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7

country_event = { #Russian Republic(TRM) breaks away!
	id = tram.98
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.98" }
	title = tram.98.t
	desc = tram.98.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #war
		name = tram.98.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = { 
					OR = {
						TRM_semyenov_in_power = yes 
						has_government = social_conservative
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -15
				TRM = {
					OR = {
						has_idea = TRM_economic_ties_to_japan_1
						has_idea = TRM_economic_ties_to_japan_2
						has_idea = TRM_economic_ties_to_japan_3
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				TRM = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = TRM_economic_ties_to_japan_1
						has_idea = TRM_economic_ties_to_japan_2
						has_idea = TRM_economic_ties_to_japan_3
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_japan_intervention option = TRM_JAPAN_INTERVENTION_FALSE }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_japan_intervention option = TRM_JAPAN_INTERVENTION_TRUE }
			}
		}
		TRM = {
			country_event = {
				id = tram.48
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #leave them
		name = tram.98.a

			base = 75
			modifier = {
				factor = 0

						has_idea = TRM_economic_ties_to_japan_3
					}
				}
			}

				add = -15
				TRM = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = TRM_economic_ties_to_japan_1
						has_idea = TRM_economic_ties_to_japan_2
						has_idea = TRM_economic_ties_to_japan_3
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_japan_intervention option = TRM_JAPAN_INTERVENTION_TRUE }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_japan_intervention option = TRM_JAPAN_INTERVENTION_FALSE }
			}
		}
		TRM = { 
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = -0.05 }
		}
	}
}

		RUS = {

				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_core_of = TRM
						state = 565
						state = 566
						state = 564
						state = 563
					}
				}
				TRM = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			country_event = tram.110
		}
		567 = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = TRM
					}
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = TRM
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = TRM
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = TRM_control_FE

		}

country_event = {
	id = tram.119
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.119" }
	title = tram.119.t
	desc = tram.119.d

	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		OR = {
			check_variable = { party_popularity@social_conservative > 0.35 }
			check_variable = { party_popularity@social_conservative = 0.35 }
		}
		TRM_has_japanese_influence = yes
		TRM_japanese_in_power = no
		TRM_semyenov_in_power = no
		NOT = {
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_idea = TRM_Grigoriy_M_Semyenov_hog_pau
			has_war = yes
			has_country_flag = TRM_delegation_bypass
			is_subject_of = JAP
		} 
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Yui Mitsue owerthrow current government
		name = tram.119.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = -0.3
		TRM_setup_japanese_gov = yes
		get_current_government_type = yes
		JAP = { puppet = TRM }
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
	}
	
	option = { #AI bypass
		name = tram.119.c
		trigger = {
			is_ai = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = TRM_japanese_ai }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = TRM_delegation_bypass
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = -0.15
		}
	}
}

	id = tram.120
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.120" }

	desc = tram.120.d

	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		OR = {
			check_variable = { party_popularity@social_conservative > 0.35 }
			check_variable = { party_popularity@social_conservative = 0.35 }
		}
		TRM_has_japanese_influence = yes
		TRM_japanese_in_power = no
		OR = {
			TRM_semyenov_in_power = yes
			has_government = social_conservative
			has_idea = TRM_Grigoriy_M_Semyenov_hog_pau
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war = yes
			has_country_flag = TRM_delegation_bypass
			is_ally_with = JAP
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Join the Japanese 
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 75			
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_forpol option = TRM_FORPOL_ON_OUR_OWN }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_forpol option = TRM_FORPOL_ENT }
				}
			}
		}
		name = tram.119.a
		JAP = { add_to_faction = ROOT }
	}

	option = { #Transamur breaks away
		name = tram.119.b
		trigger = {
			TRM = { NOT = { is_subject_of = JAP } }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25						
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_forpol option = TRM_FORPOL_JAP }
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		if = {

					TRM_remove_japanese_influence = yes

				}

					diplomatic_relation = {
						country = TRM
						relation = docking_rights
						active = no
					}
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram.150
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.122
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.122" }
	title = tram.122.t
	desc = tram.122.d

	trigger = {
		AND = {
			tag = TRM
			country_exists = RUS
			RUS = {
				has_stability < -0
				} #Will recieve some bonuses from time to time till Russia is in disturbance
			has_political_power > 0
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		months = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.122.a
		set_temp_variable_to_random = {
			var = TRM_manpower
			min = 2000
			max = 4000
		}
		add_manpower = var:TRM_manpower
		set_temp_variable_to_random = {
			var = TRM_equipment
			min = 100
			max = 250
		}
		add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
			type = infantry_equipment_1
			amount = var:TRM_equipment
			producer = RUS
		}
		set_temp_variable = { change_morale = 0.03 }
		RUS_change_siberian_war_morale = yes
	}
}

	desc = tram.123.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = tram.123.a

		custom_effect_tooltip = TRM_agitation_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				15 = {
					set_country_flag = TRM_good_agitation
				}

				40 = {
					set_country_flag = TRM_agitation
				}

				45 = {
					set_country_flag = TRM_bad_agitation
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = tram.124 days = 7 random_days = 14 }
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_country_flag = TRM_no_agitation
		set_temp_variable = { change_morale = -0.03 }
		RUS_change_siberian_war_morale = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.123.b
		set_country_flag = TRM_no_agitation
		set_temp_variable = { change_morale = 0.05 }
		RUS_change_siberian_war_morale = yes
	}

			}
		}

			}

				}

	}

			}
		}
	}

###TRM - Entente negotiations outcome###
country_event = {
	id = tram.127
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.127" }
	title = tram.127.t
	desc = {
		text = tram.127.fullsupport
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = TRM_entente_full_support
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = tram.127.partialsupport
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = TRM_entente_partial_support
		}
	}

	desc = {
		text = tram.127.nosupport
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = TRM_entente_no_support
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Full support
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = TRM_entente_full_support
		}
		name = tram.127.a
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = -0.04 }
		every_owned_state = { 
			limit = { TRM_is_legitimate_state = yes }
			TRM_Increase_Kolchak_Support = yes 
		}
		add_political_power = 40
		FROM = {
			every_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_unit_leader_flag = CAN_TRM_expedition_leader }
				set_nationality = TRM
				remove_unit_leader_trait = GBR_british_exile_trait
				add_unit_leader_trait = TRM_british_expeditionary
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 1514 }
				set_nationality = JAP
			}
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENT decision = TRM_Seek_For_Entente_Support }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENT decision = TRM_Open_British_Embassy }
	}

	option = { #Partial support
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = TRM_entente_partial_support
		}
		name = tram.127.b
		add_political_power = 20
		add_popularity = {ideology = social_conservative popularity = -0.04 }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENT decision = TRM_Seek_For_Entente_Support }		
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ENT decision = TRM_Open_British_Embassy }
	}

	option = { #No support
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = TRM_entente_no_support
		}
		name = tram.127.c
		every_owned_state = { 
			limit = { TRM_is_legitimate_state = yes }
			TRM_Decrease_Kolchak_Support = yes 
		}
		add_popularity = {ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.01 }
		add_popularity = {ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.02 }
	}
}

###Mission-based peace deal with Japan###
country_event = {
	id = tram.128
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.128" }
	title = tram.128.t
	desc = tram.128.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = tram.128.trm
		trigger = {
			tag = TRM
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = JAP
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = tram.128.jap
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					408 = { 
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_owned_by = TRM
					}
					1246 = { 
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_owned_by = TRM
					}
					409 = { 
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_owned_by = TRM
					}
				}
			}
			TRM = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 408
							state = 1246
							state = 409
						}
					}
					transfer_state_to = JAP
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			TRM = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = TRM
				}
				remove_claim_by = JAP
				transfer_state_to = TRM
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					537 = { is_controlled_by = TRM }
				}
				537 = { transfer_state_to = TRM }
			}
		}

	}
}

	desc = tram.145.d

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = TRM_dream }

				remove_idea = TRM_dream
				add_idea = TRM_dream_fulfilled
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = TRM_dream_fulfilled
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_russian_starting_claims = yes 
				has_resistance = yes
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
			add_compliance = 10
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Unrest in Chita
	id = trmnra.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event trmnra.1" }	
	title = trmnra.1.t
	desc = trmnra.1.d

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		check_variable = { TRM_Overall_NRA_Resistance > 0.199 }
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
		}
		name = trmnra.1.a
		657 = {
			damage_building = {
				type = industrial_complex
				damage = 0.50
			}
			damage_building = {
				type = infrastructure
				damage = 0.25
			}
			TRM_Increase_NRA_Resistance = yes 
		}
		add_stability = -0.2
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.05			
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = trmnra.2
				days = 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #AI bypass
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ai = yes
			NOT = { 
				has_country_flag = TRM_nra_ai 
				has_country_flag = TRM_czechs_ai 
				has_country_flag = TRM_czechs_panslavist_ai 
			}
		}
		name = trmnra.1.b

			}
		}
		else_if = {

					SOV_any_bolshevik_in_power = yes
				}
			}

		}
		add_tot_to_coalition = yes
		add_synd_to_coalition = yes
	}
	option = {

		trigger = {

				NOT = { has_country_leader = { name = "Martemyan Ryutin" ruling_only = yes } }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {

				factor = 0

					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_nra_third_congress option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP_SYNDIE }

		}

		}

			}

			limit = { is_siberia = yes }

			SOV_puppet_ROOT_effect = yes

		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 1955 }

				id = russia.1925

			}

		}

			set_nationality = FROM
		}

			}

country_event = {
	id = trmnra.106
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event trmnra.106" }
	title = trmnra.106.t
	desc = {
		text = trmnra.106.d
		trigger = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
	}
	desc = {
		text = trmnra.106.d2
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
		}
	}
	
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		TRM_nra_in_power = yes
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = trmnra.106.a
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_nra_third_congress option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = TRM_path option = RULE_OPTION_TRM_NRA_COUP }
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_siberia = yes
					is_central_asia = yes
				}
				NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
				is_owned_by = FROM
			}
			transfer_state_to = ROOT
			if = {
				limit = { is_siberia = yes }
				remove_core_of = FROM
				add_claim_by = FROM
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
						}
						ROOT = { divisions_in_state = { state = PREV size > 0 } }
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = { tag = ROOT }
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = ROOT
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
				}
			}
			remove_puppet_and_leave_faction = yes
		}		
		add_ideas = TRM_dream
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_core_of = RUS
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}		
		FROM = {
			country_event = trmnra.105
		}		
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = TRM_SOV }
			set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_NRA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 1 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 2 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_political_power = -30
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 3 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.15
			add_political_power = -60

country_event = {
	id = trmnra.107
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event trmnra.107" }
	title = trmnra.107.t
	desc = trmnra.107.d
	
	trigger = {
		tag = TRM
		TRM_nra_in_power = yes
	}
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = trmnra.107.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_siberia = yes
					is_central_asia = yes
				}
				NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
				is_owned_by = FROM
			}
			transfer_state_to = ROOT
			if = {
				limit = { is_siberia = yes }
				remove_core_of = FROM
				add_claim_by = FROM
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = FROM }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							is_owned_by = ROOT
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
						}
						ROOT = { divisions_in_state = { state = PREV size > 0 } }
					}
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = { tag = ROOT }
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					teleport_armies = {
						limit = {
							NOT = {
								tag = ROOT
								has_war_with = ROOT
							}
						}
						to_state_array = owned_controlled_states
					}
				}
			}
			remove_puppet_and_leave_faction = yes
		}		
		add_ideas = TRM_dream
		every_state = {
			limit = { 
				is_core_of = RUS
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = trmnra.105
		}		
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = TRM_SOV }
			set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_NRA
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 1 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_political_power = -15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 2 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_political_power = -30
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { RUS_Speech_About_Peaceful_Unification_amount_var = 3 }
			}
			add_stability = -0.15
			add_political_power = -60
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = TRM }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #
		name = trmnra.106.c
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = FROM
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = trmnra.111
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event trmnra.111" }
	title = trmnra.111.t
	desc = trmnra.111.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #
		name = trmnra.111.a		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_politburo_established
				NOT = { has_country_flag = SOV_politburo_dissolved }
				OR = {
					nsp_in_power = yes
					has_government = totalist
					AND = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = SOV_congress_elections_after_nep
							has_country_flag = SOV_congress_elections_after_nep_success
						}
						has_country_leader = { name = "Congress of Soviets" ruling_only = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Pyetr Nikiforov"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { politburo_change = 2 }
				SOV_change_politburo_left_communists = yes	
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_leader = {
							name = "Yemelyan Yaroslavsky"
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { politburo_change = 2 }
				SOV_change_politburo_hardliners = yes		
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						OR = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Nikolay Kalashnikov"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Yevgeniy Kolosov"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { politburo_change = 2 }
				SOV_change_politburo_kirov = yes	
			}
			else = {
				set_temp_variable = { politburo_change = 2 }
				SOV_change_politburo_bukharin = yes
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SOV_congress_ongoing
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						OR = {
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Nikolay Kalashnikov"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
							has_country_leader = {
								name = "Yevgeniy Kolosov"
								ruling_only = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				SOV_soviet_congress_increase_plsr = yes
				SOV_soviet_congress_increase_psr = yes
				SOV_soviet_congress_increase_rsdrp = yes
			}
			else = {			
				SOV_soviet_congress_increase_nsp = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

			base = 50
		}

		add_ideas = TRM_Sergey_Taskin_hog_mli
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.02 }
		country_event = { id = tramsem.18 days = 5 }
	}
	option = {
		name = tramsem.11.b	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = TRM_semyonov_change_pataut
		hidden_effect = {
			set_politics = { ruling_party = paternal_autocrat }
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				name = TRM_authoritarian_democrat_party
				long_name = TRM_authoritarian_democrat_party_long
			}			
			set_temp_variable = { TRM_new_pataut = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
			add_to_temp_variable = { TRM_new_pataut = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat  }

			set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = TRM_new_pataut }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

			add_to_temp_variable = { TRM_new_pataut = sum } #avoid rounding errors

			set_popularities = {
				totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
				syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
				radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
				social_democrat = party_popularity_100@social_democrat
				social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
				market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
				social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
				authoritarian_democrat = 0
				paternal_autocrat = TRM_new_pataut
				national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = { TRM_semyenov_in_power = no }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Grigory Semyonov"
					desc = "POLITICS_SEMYONOV_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Grigory_Semyonov.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = pataut_cossack_subtype
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = TRM_All_Power_From_Chita }
					add_country_leader_trait = RUS_ataman_of_east
				}
			}
		}
		country_event = { id = tramsem.18 days = 5 }
	}
}

news_event = { #Kolchak dead
	id = tramnews.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tramnews.1" }
	title = tramnews.1.t
	desc = tramnews.1.d
	picture = GFX_news_event_TRM_kolchak

	major = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	show_major = {
		NOT = {
			tag = TRM
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = tramnews.1.a
		trigger = { original_tag = JAP }
	}
	option = {
		name = tramnews.1.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { original_tag = JAP }
			OR = {
				is_ally_with = TRM
				original_tag = ORE
				original_tag = URL
				original_tag = RVA
				original_tag = WRA
				AND = {
					original_tag = RUS
					OR = {
						has_right_democratic_government = yes
						has_authoritarian_government = yes
					}
					has_non_aggression_pact_with = TRM
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tramnews.1.c
		trigger = {
			original_tag = RUS
			has_right_democratic_government = no
			has_authoritarian_government = no
			NOT = { has_non_aggression_pact_with = TRM }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tramnews.1.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_ally_with = TRM
				original_tag = JAP 
				original_tag = ORE
				original_tag = URL
				original_tag = RVA
				original_tag = WRA
				original_tag = RUS
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = trammlad.515
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event trammlad.515"}
	title = trammlad.515.t
	desc = trammlad.515.d
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { 
		name = trammlad.515.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_nats
		remove_all_ministers = yes
		add_ideas = {
			TRM_Anastasiy_Vonsyatsky_hog_npo
			TRM_Arseniy_Nesmelov_for_npo
			TRM_Lev_Okhotin_eco_npo
			TRM_Mikhail_Matkovsky_sec_npo
		}
		TRM_swap_legitimacy = yes
		set_country_flag = TRM_Nats_in_power
		clr_country_flag = TRM_Mlad_in_power
		remove_ideas = TRM_tsar_soviets_idea
		effect_tooltip = { unlock_national_focus = TRM_Nationalists_Take_Over }
		XXA = {
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = { has_id = 243801 }
				set_nationality = ROOT
				promote_to_marshal = yes
			}
		}
		random_unit_leader = {
			limit = { has_id = 243800 }
			add_skill_level = 1 
			add_max_trait = 1
		}
		hidden_effect = { 
			complete_national_focus = TRM_Nationalists_Take_Over
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mladorossi Leadership Council"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Regency.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"
				ideology = mladorossi_subtype
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TRM_new_totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist }
			divide_temp_variable = { TRM_new_totalist = 2 }

			set_temp_variable = { TRM_new_natpop = party_popularity_100@national_populist }
			add_to_temp_variable = { TRM_new_natpop = TRM_new_totalist }

			set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = TRM_new_totalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = TRM_new_natpop }

			add_to_temp_variable = { TRM_new_natpop = sum } #avoid rounding errors

			set_popularities = {
				totalist = TRM_new_totalist
				syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
				radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
				social_democrat = party_popularity_100@social_democrat
				social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
				market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
				social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
				authoritarian_democrat = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat
				paternal_autocrat = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat
				national_populist = TRM_new_natpop
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Kirill I"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = TRM_restore_nat
		}			
	}
}

		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			name = TRM_totalist_party
			long_name = TRM_Mlad_party_socdem_long
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.1 }
		add_socdem_to_coalition = yes
		if = {
			limit = { RUS_russian_monarch = yes }

				limit = { RUS_tsar_vladimir = yes }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Vladimir III"
					desc = "POLITICS_VLADIMIR_ROMANOV_CON_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Vladimir_III.png"

					ideology = socdem_mladorossi_subtype
					traits = { RUS_tsar_of_all_russia peoples_tsar }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { RUS_tsar_kirill = yes }
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Kirill I"
					desc = "POLITICS_KYRIL_ROMANOV_MLAD_DESC"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Tsar_Kyril.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_mladorossi_subtype
					traits = { RUS_tsar_of_all_russia RUS_self_proclaimed_emperor peoples_tsar }
				}
			}
			else = {
				create_country_leader = {
					name = "Nikita I"
					picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Nikita_Aleksandrovich.png"
					expire = "1.1.1"
					ideology = socdem_mladorossi_subtype
					traits = { RUS_tsar_of_all_russia peoples_tsar }
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Mladorossi Regency Council"
				desc = "POLITICS_REGENCY_COUNCIL_RUSSIA_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Regency.png"
				expire = "1.1.1"

country_event = {
	id = tram.221
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.221" }
	
	title = uch.23.t
	desc = tram.221.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = uch.23.a
		decrease_ruling_party_popularity_by_10 = yes
		add_stability = -0.10
	}
	option = {
		name = uch.23.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = RUS_socialist_resistance
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_socialist_resistance
				add_idea = RUS_socialist_resistance_1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = RUS_socialist_resistance_1
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_socialist_resistance_1
				add_idea = RUS_socialist_resistance_2
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_ideas = RUS_socialist_resistance_2
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			name = TRM_social_democrat_kolchak
			long_name = TRM_social_democrat_kolchak_long
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			name = TRM_social_democrat_kolchak
			long_name = TRM_social_democrat_kolchak_long
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Georgy Gins"
			desc = "POLITICS_GINS_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Gins.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = radsoc_popular_patriotism_subtype
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			name = "Georgy Gins"
			desc = "POLITICS_GINS_DESC"
			picture = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Gins.png"
			expire = "1.1.1"
			ideology = popular_patriotism_subtype
		}		
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { UCH_new_socdem = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
			add_to_temp_variable = { UCH_new_socdem = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist  }
			add_to_temp_variable = { UCH_new_socdem = party_popularity_100@syndicalist  }
			add_to_temp_variable = { UCH_new_socdem = party_popularity_100@totalist  }

			set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = UCH_new_socdem }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

			add_to_temp_variable = { UCH_new_socdem = sum } #avoid rounding errors

			set_popularities = {
				totalist = 0
				syndicalist = 0
				radical_socialist = 0
				social_democrat = UCH_new_socdem
				social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
				market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
				social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
				authoritarian_democrat = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat
				paternal_autocrat = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat
				national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram.226
	immediate = { 
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram.226" 
		hidden_effect = {
			every_possible_country = {
				limit = { 
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					OR = {
						is_central_asian_tag = yes
						original_tag = DKB
						original_tag = KUB
						original_tag = KLY
						original_tag = MTR
						original_tag = GEO
						original_tag = AZE
						original_tag = ARM
						original_tag = CRM
						original_tag = MON
						original_tag = KAR
					}
				}
				ROOT = { activate_targeted_decision = { target = PREV decision = RUS_Attack_Country_default } }
			}
		}
	}
	title = tram.226.t
	desc = tram.226.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = tram.226.a
		add_political_power = 250
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = -0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_post_pepelyaev }
			if = { 
				limit = { has_idea = TRM_big_federation }
				set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_PEPEL_RUS_usa
			}
			else = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_PEPEL_RUS_fed
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = TRM_PROV }
			set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_RUS
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			name = RUS_sgor_party
			long_name = RUS_sgor_party_long
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			name = RUS_sgor_party
			long_name = RUS_sgor_party_long
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_coalition_with_authoritarian_democrat = no }
			add_authdem_to_coalition = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_in_coalition_with_paternal_autocrat = no }
			add_pataut_to_coalition = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { 
					has_country_leader_with_trait = RUS_supreme_ruler 
					has_country_leader_with_trait = RUS_supreme_ataman 
					has_country_leader_with_trait = RUS_ataman_of_east 
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_trait = RUS_supreme_ruler
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TRM_semyenov_in_power = yes }
			remove_ideas_with_trait = head_of_government
			add_ideas = TRM_Sergey_Taskin_hog_mli
			set_country_leader_portrait = {
				portrait = "gfx/leaders/TRM/Portrait_TRM_Grigory_Semyonov_civilian.png"
			}
		}
		add_ideas = {
			RUS_monarchist_resistance
			RUS_democrat_resistance
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = { 
				ideology = syndicalist
				name = SOV_rtssps_party
				long_name = SOV_rtssps_party_long
			}
		}
	}
}

		add_to_variable = { TRM_sgor = 1 }
		add_stability = 0.05		
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = RUS_socialist_resistance
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = RUS_socialist_resistance

			}

		else_if = {

			}

			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_ideas = RUS_socialist_resistance_2
		}

			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }

			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_post_pepelyaev }
			set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_PEPEL_RUS
		}
		else = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = TRM_RUS
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = { TRM_nps > TRM_sgor }
				check_variable = { TRM_nps > TRM_psr }
			}
			set_politics = { ruling_party = market_liberal }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_post_pepelyaev } }
				add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
				add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.20 }
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				TRM_Viktor_N_Pepelyayev_hog_mli
				TRM_Nikolay_Uhtomsky_for_mli
				TRM_Stepan_V_Vostrotin_eco_mli
				TRM_Leonid_A_Ustrugov_sec_mli
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { 
				check_variable = { TRM_psr > TRM_sgor }
				check_variable = { TRM_psr > TRM_nps }
			}
			set_politics = { ruling_party = social_democrat }
			add_radsoc_to_coalition = yes
			add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
			add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.20 }
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				TRM_Florian_Fedorovich_hog_sde
				TRM_Mikhail_B_Shatila_for_sde
				TRM_Vladimir_M_Krutovsky_eco_sde
				TRM_Alexander_E_Novoselov_sec_sde
			}
		}
		else = {			
			set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat }		
			add_pataut_to_coalition = yes
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = RUS_post_pepelyaev }
				add_soclib_to_coalition = yes
				add_soccon_to_coalition = yes
			}
			add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.10 }
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = {
				TRM_Viktor_N_Pepelyayev_hog_mli
				TRM_Nikolay_Uhtomsky_for_mli
				TRM_Ivan_Adrianovich_Mikhailov_eco_pau
				TRM_Leonid_A_Ustrugov_sec_mli
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

		}

			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.3
				has_stability > 0.2
			}
			add_stability = 0.25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.4
				has_stability > 0.3
			}
			add_stability = 0.2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.5
				has_stability > 0.4
			}
			add_stability = 0.15
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_support < 0.5
			}
			add_war_support = 0.15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.6
				has_stability > 0.5
			}
			add_stability = 0.1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.7
				has_stability > 0.6
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_stability > 0.7
				has_stability < 1
			}

			}
			add_resistance = -20
			add_compliance = 30
		}

		activate_targeted_decision = { target = ORE decision = TRM_expand_south }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = URL decision = TRM_expand_south }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = BKN decision = TRM_expand_south }

			566 = {
				owner = { country_event = tram_crisis_1936.2 }
			}
		}
	}
	title = tram_crisis_1936.1.t
	desc = tram_crisis_1936.1.d

	}
}

country_event = {
	id = tram_crisis_1937.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event tram_crisis_1937.5" }
	title = tram_crisis_1937.5.t
	desc = tram_crisis_1937.5.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = TRM
		owns_state = 564
		NOT = { 
			owns_state = 566
			has_war_with = var:566.owner 
			is_ally_with = var:566.owner
		}
	}
		
	option = {
		name = tram_crisis_1937.5.a
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = prepare_for_war
			id = FROM
			value = -1000
		}
		FROM = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = prepare_for_war
				id = FROM
				value = -1000
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = TRM_anti_air_defences
					has_country_flag = TRM_border_control
				}
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1937.6
					days = 5
					random_days = 7
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					count_triggers = {
						amount = 1
						has_country_flag = TRM_anti_air_defences
						has_country_flag = TRM_border_control
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1937.8
					days = 5
					random_days = 7
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1937.7
					days = 5
					random_days = 7
				}
			}
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = RUS }
					NOT = { tag = TRM }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = tram_crisis_1937.16
					days = 5
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				add_named_threat = {
					threat = 1
					name = tram_crisis_1937.16.t
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = tram_crisis_1937.5.b
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { russian_civil_war = no }
				OR = {
					GER = { has_war_with = RUS }
					INT = { has_war_with = RUS }
					JAP = { has_war_with = RUS }
					ENT = { has_war_with = RUS }
					has_country_flag = TRM_decision_to_attack_russia
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_owner_neighbor_of = FROM
				any_allied_country = { is_owner_neighbor_of = FROM }
				has_idea = TRM_dream
				has_idea = TRM_Sib_Fed
				has_idea = TRM_cossackia
			}
			NOT = { 
				has_non_aggression_pact_with = FROM 
				has_country_flag = RUS_negotiating_siberia
				has_active_mission = TRM_will_declare_war_on_RUS
			}
			can_declare_war_on = FROM
			if = {
				limit = { russian_civil_war = no }
				FROM = { owns_state = 219 }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				russian_civil_war = no
				OR = {
					RUS_dont_attack_if_vulnerable_or_preparing = yes
					FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_target_is_stronger = yes }
					FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_faction_is_stronger = yes }
					FROM = { RUS_dont_attack_if_overlord_is_stronger = yes }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				AND = {
					russian_civil_war = yes
					FROM = { tag = RUS }
					TRM_nra_game_rule = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				russian_civil_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				TRM = { has_country_flag = TRM_integration_with_russia }
			}
		}
		add_ai_strategy = {
			type = prepare_for_war
			id = FROM
			value = -1000
		}
		FROM = {
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = prepare_for_war
				id = FROM
				value = -1000
			}
		}	
		set_country_flag = TRM_decision_to_attack_russia		
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = annex_everything
		}
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = TRM_for_russia
			days = 365
		}
		set_country_flag = TRM_has_attacked_@FROM
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = TRM }
				}
				news_event = {
					id = russianews.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
